msg:The service attitude is really bad... I stayed here once when it first opened, and the experience was really good. When we checked out, the manager came to ask us how our stay was and did you have any suggestions? This time it was really The service experience is so bad. Everything about the hotel facilities and environment is very good, but the service is really hard to say... My partner came early to surprise him with a room for his birthday, so I was the only one who filled in the check-in information. When I returned to the hotel in the evening , the staff at the door kept asking us if we were staying in the hotel and which room we were staying in. We answered that it seemed to be room xxx, and then the person at the door said "Don't be like this" and then we told you to show you the room card, and then Just left. While waiting for the elevator, we noticed that five or six staff at the front desk were staring at us, and then asked us to go back and register. This is understandable. Indeed, the epidemic prevention work is very strict now. After we passed, four or five people surrounded us and asked us. What if we only registered one person? It was really embarrassing. Then after we started to register, the staff started to tell the security guard loudly that we were not registered and pointed at us. It was really speechless. The problem is that we didn't want to register. When we walked in, we were asked four or five times whether we were staying in which room in the hotel. After answering, we left as usual... I have stayed in many five-star hotels in Yiwu before. The service in this hotel is really the worst. I spent my birthday at Universal last year. There was no cleaning fee for the balloons and other decorations. I stayed here this year and was charged a cleaning fee of 200 yuan when I checked out.
